  260     -- Signals
  261     SIGNAL addr_B_unsigned                  : unsigned(9 DOWNTO 0);  -- ufix10
  262     SIGNAL convertB_out1                    : unsigned(15 DOWNTO 0);  -- uint16
  263     SIGNAL ram_data_B_out1                  : unsigned(15 DOWNTO 0);  -- uint16
  264     SIGNAL And_out1                         : std_logic;
  265     SIGNAL din_A_signed                     : signed(63 DOWNTO 0);  -- sfix64_En32
  266     SIGNAL addr_A_unsigned                  : unsigned(9 DOWNTO 0);  -- ufix10
  267     SIGNAL convertA_out1                    : unsigned(15 DOWNTO 0);  -- uint16
  268     SIGNAL din_B_signed                     : signed(63 DOWNTO 0);  -- sfix64_En32
  269     SIGNAL switch_A_out1                    : vector_of_signed64(0 TO 1023);  -- sfix64_En32 [1024]
  270     SIGNAL wr_port1_out1                    : vector_of_signed64(0 TO 1023);  -- sfix64_En32 [1024]
  271     SIGNAL ram_out1                         : vector_of_signed64(0 TO 1023);  -- sfix64_En32 [1024]
  272     SIGNAL wr_port_out1                     : vector_of_signed64(0 TO 1023);  -- sfix64_En32 [1024]
  273     SIGNAL switch_A2_out1                   : vector_of_signed64(0 TO 1023);  -- sfix64_En32 [1024]
  274     SIGNAL switch_B_out1                    : vector_of_signed64(0 TO 1023);  -- sfix64_En32 [1024]
  275     SIGNAL select_B_out1                    : signed(63 DOWNTO 0);  -- sfix64_En32
  276     SIGNAL Data_Type_Conversion_Inherited_B_out1 : std_logic_vector(63 DOWNTO 0);  -- ufix64
  277     SIGNAL ram_data_A_out1                  : unsigned(15 DOWNTO 0);  -- uint16
  278     SIGNAL select_A_out1                    : signed(63 DOWNTO 0);  -- sfix64_En32
  279     SIGNAL Data_Type_Conversion_Inherited_A_out1 : std_logic_vector(63 DOWNTO 0);  -- ufix64
  280   
  281   BEGIN
  282     -- '<S697>/Data Type Conversion Inherited B'
  283     u_Data_Type_Conversion_Inherited_B : sm_DynamicCompression_Data_Type_Conversion_Inherited_B_block4
  284       PORT MAP( u => std_logic_vector(select_B_out1),  -- sfix64_En32
  285                 y => Data_Type_Conversion_Inherited_B_out1  -- sfix64_En32
  286                 );
  287   
  288     -- '<S697>/Data Type Conversion Inherited A'
  289     u_Data_Type_Conversion_Inherited_A : sm_DynamicCompression_Data_Type_Conversion_Inherited_A_block4

  299   
  300     -- '<S697>/ram_data_B'
  301     ram_data_B_process : PROCESS (clk, reset)
  302     BEGIN
  303       IF reset = '1' THEN
  304         ram_data_B_out1 <= to_unsigned(16#0000#, 16);
  305       ELSIF rising_edge(clk) THEN
  306         IF enb = '1' THEN
  307           ram_data_B_out1 <= convertB_out1;
  308         END IF;
  309       END IF;
  310     END PROCESS ram_data_B_process;

 6474     -- '<S697>/switch_A'
 6475

 6477         wr_port_out1;

 6482         wr_port1_out1;

 6487         switch_A2_out1;
 6488   
 6489     -- '<S697>/ram'
 6490     ram_process : PROCESS (clk, reset)
 6491     BEGIN
 6492       IF reset = '1' THEN
 6493         ram_out1 <= ram_data;
 6494       ELSIF rising_edge(clk) THEN
 6495         IF enb = '1' THEN
 6496           ram_out1 <= switch_B_out1;
 6497         END IF;
 6498       END IF;
 6499     END PROCESS ram_process;
 6500   
 6501

 6503   
 6504     select_B_out1 <= ram_out1(to_integer(ram_data_B_out1)) WHEN ram_data_B_out1 <= to_unsigned(16#03FF#, 16) ELSE
 6505         ram_out1(1023);
 6506

 6508   
 6509     -- '<S697>/Data Type Duplicate1'
 6510   
 6511     -- '<S697>/ram_data_A'
 6512     ram_data_A_process : PROCESS (clk, reset)
 6513     BEGIN
 6514       IF reset = '1' THEN
 6515         ram_data_A_out1 <= to_unsigned(16#0000#, 16);
 6516       ELSIF rising_edge(clk) THEN
 6517         IF enb = '1' THEN
 6518           ram_data_A_out1 <= convertA_out1;
 6519         END IF;
 6520       END IF;
 6521     END PROCESS ram_data_A_process;
 6522   
 6523

 6525   
 6526     select_A_out1 <= ram_out1(to_integer(ram_data_A_out1)) WHEN ram_data_A_out1 <= to_unsigned(16#03FF#, 16) ELSE
 6527         ram_out1(1023);
 6528   
 6529     dout_B <= Data_Type_Conversion_Inherited_B_out1;
